route-policy DENY_ALL
  drop
end-policy
!
route-policy pass-all
  pass
end-policy
!
route-policy Allow_All
  pass
end-policy
!
route-policy E_RAN_OM_IN
  if ((extcommunity rt matches-any E_RAN_OM-Import_RT) and (destination in PFX_E_RAN_OM_IN)) then
    drop
  else
    pass
  endif
end-policy
!
route-policy ENT_CPE_OM_OUT
  if destination in ENT_CPE_OM_MESINIAGA_Pfx then
    pass
  else
    drop
  endif
end-policy
!
route-policy set_locpref300
  set local-preference 300
end-policy
!
route-policy E_2G3G-Export-RT
  if destination in E_RNC_BSC_KPG_Pfx then
    set extcommunity rt E_2G3G_HUB_KPG_RT additive
    set extcommunity rt E_2G3G_OM_SPOKE_RT additive
    set extcommunity rt E_2G3G_SERVICE_RT additive
  elseif destination in E_RAN_KPGAGGA02_Pfx then
    set extcommunity rt E_2G3G_OM_SPOKE_RT additive
    set extcommunity rt E_2G3G_SERVICE_RT additive
  elseif destination in E_PTP_GM_Ctrl_Pfx then
    set extcommunity rt E_2G3G_SERVICE_RT additive
  elseif destination in E_KPRN51_BSC15_Pfx then
    set extcommunity rt E_2G3G_HUB_KPG_RT additive
    set extcommunity rt E_2G3G_SERVICE_RT additive
  elseif destination in E_2G3G_NODEB_VSAT_Pfx then
    set extcommunity rt E_2G3G_HUB_ATB_RT additive
    set extcommunity rt E_2G3G_OM_SPOKE_RT additive
    set extcommunity rt E_2G3G_SERVICE_RT additive
  endif
end-policy
!
route-policy H_2G3G-Export-RT
  if destination in H_2G3G_NODEB_VSAT_Pfx then
    set extcommunity rt H_2G3G_HUB_ATB_RT additive
  elseif destination in H_2G3G_OM_VSAT_Pfx then
    set extcommunity rt H_2G3G_OM_SPOKE_RT additive
  elseif destination in PTN_MOCN_RNC_BSC_Pfx then
    set extcommunity rt H_2G3G_KPG_HUB_RT additive
  elseif destination in CD_ABIS_HW_BSC_Central then
    set extcommunity rt (65535:25030) additive
  elseif destination in CD_ABIS_HW_BSC_Eastern then
    set extcommunity rt (65535:25030) additive
  endif
end-policy
!
route-policy VRF_Gb_Export_RT
  if (destination in Gb_MOCN_RAN) then
    set extcommunity rt (65535:66401) additive
  endif
end-policy
!
route-policy redist_loopback0
  if destination in (10.240.100.253/32) then
    pass
  else
    drop
  endif
end-policy
!
route-policy PREFER-ACC-ROUTES
  set weight 10000
end-policy
!
route-policy ospf-spf-priority
  if (destination in ospf-high-prefixes) then
    set spf-priority high
  endif
end-policy
!
route-policy E_CS_IuR-Export-RT
  if (destination in E_CS_IuR-RT) then
    set extcommunity rt (65535:60481, 65535:60389) additive
  endif
end-policy
!

    set extcommunity rt (65535:60362) additive
  endif
end-policy
!
route-policy E_2G3G-EGRESS_FILTER
  if destination in DEFAULT then
    drop
  elseif destination in E_RNC_VSAT_Pfx then
    pass
  elseif destination in E_PTP_KPG_Pfx then
    pass
  elseif destination in E_RNC_BSC_SHT_Pfx then
    drop
  elseif destination in E_NMS_Pfx then
    drop
  elseif extcommunity rt matches-any Eastern_E_RT then
    drop
  else
    pass
  endif
end-policy
!

  set path-selection backup 1 install multipath-protect advertise
end-policy

  remote-as 65535
  password encrypted xxxxxxxx

  update-source Loopback0
  address-family vpnv4 unicast

  address-family vpnv6 unicast
  !
  address-family ipv4 rt-filter
  !

  !

   route-policy DENY_ALL in
   next-hop-self
  !
 !

  remote-as 65535
  password encrypted xxxxxxxx
  description T-RR and S-RR client
  update-source Loopback0
  address-family vpnv4 unicast
   route-policy PREFER-ACC-ROUTES in
   route-reflector-client
  !
  address-family vpnv6 unicast
   route-policy PREFER-ACC-ROUTES in
   route-reflector-client
  !

   route-policy PREFER-ACC-ROUTES in
   route-reflector-client
   default-originate

  address-family l2vpn evpn
   route-reflector-client
